<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сковывать.html>ско́вывать</a> (17803)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковывать.html>ско́вывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skóvyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to forge, to hammer out</li>
<li>to forge together</li>
<li>to chain</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hold, to fix
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сковывать.html>ско́вывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>огнём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skóvyvatʹ</b> ognjóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pin (down) by fire</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(with ice)</i> to lock</li>
<li>to fetter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>страх</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">strax <b>skovál</b> mne dúšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I was overcome/seized with fear</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сковывать.html>ско́вывающий</a> (17803)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковывать.html>ско́вывающий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skóvyvajuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковывать.html>ско́вывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skóvyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колотить.html>колоти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скольжение.html>скольже́ние</a> (24714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skolʹzítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скольжение.html>скольже́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skolʹžénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скольжение.html>скольже́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скольжение.html>скольже́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скольжение.html>скольже́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sliding, slipping, slippage</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользи́ть</a> (4615)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ско́льз(<a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a>)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skólʹz(kij)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skolʹzítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользнуть.html>скользну́ть</a></b>)

***скользкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скользкий.html>ско́льзкий</a> (5576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*ко́льзкий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*kólʹzkij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slippery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ко́льзко</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kólʹzko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is attested), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">кользъкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolĭzŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">сковзки́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skovzkýj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slippery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">ко́взати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kóvzaty</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to slip</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Additionally cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kiełzać</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stumble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Per Vasmer, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kъlz-</i>, of unknown further origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользкий.html>ско́льзкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skólʹzkij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ско́льзче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>slippery, dangerous <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a surface</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>slimy</li></ol>

***скользнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скользнуть.html>скользну́ть</a> (5021)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">скълъзнути</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skŭlŭznuti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically derived from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skolʹzítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользнуть.html>скользну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skolʹznútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to slide, to slip</li>
<li>to glide</li>
<li>to float</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sneak <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">into, by</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to graze <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative, someone/something; of a bullet</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><b>скольз<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользи́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-скольз-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ну</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">колико</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koliko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*koliko</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skólʹko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>how much, how many

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Skólʹko</b> u vas knig?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How many books do you have?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Skólʹko</b> vam let?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How old are you?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́льких</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:умереть.html>у́мер</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Skólʹkix</b> let on úmer?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">At what age did he die?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>so much, so many

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколь.html>ско́ль</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a></b>
</p><p>Числительное, местоименное <a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>наре́чие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:союзный.html>сою́зное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопросительный.html>вопроси́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>употребля́ется</a> разг. <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> р.п. <i>скольки́</i>: <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> скольки, <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> скольки.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выражение.html>выраже́ниях</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́па</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> т. п.) <a href = vnd.unilang:наряд.html>наря́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмой</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> <i>ско́льку</i>. 
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-скольк-</b>; суффикс: <b>-о</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***скончаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скончаться.html>сконча́ться</a> (6984)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сконча́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skončátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скончаться.html>сконча́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skončátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pass away <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to die, to stop living</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
